 lekin,kya aisa karnaa surakshitahai-swine flu ko lekar soshal media main aae ye ayurvedic formule-01
 Grind camphor, small cardamom and cloves or cinnamon in equal quantity
 or kapade main baandhakar uski choti si potli banaakar saath rakhen
 Keep smelling it every half an hour
 02
 Boil 4-5 leaves of basil, 5 grams of ginger, a pinch of black pepper powder and the same turmeric in a cup of water or tea and drink it two or three times a day
 03
 Drink Giloy (amrita) Bell's stem by boiling or filtering it in water
 yaa giloi satv do ratti yani chauthai gram pauna gilaas pani ke saath len
 04
 tulsi ke 5-6 pattey or kaali mirch ke 2-3 dane piskar chaay main daalkar din main do-teen baar pien
 05
 aadha chammach haldi pauna gilaas doodh main ubalkar pien
 Half a teaspoon of turmeric can also be taken by mixing it with warm water or honey
 06
 Drink half a teaspoon of amla powder in half a cup of water and drink it twice a day
 yaa tulsi patr evam aajnaghas (jarankush) ubalkar pien
 07
 dalacheenee churna shahad ke saath athwa dalacheenee kii chaay bhi laabhadaayak he
 a mixture of herbs like Giloy, Kalamedha, Chirayata, bhuin-amla, Sarpunkha, Vasa is also beneficial
 kitne kargar hai ayurveda formule?yah sawaal kai logon ke man main he

 ye swine flu hi nahin balki sabhi tarah ke hanikaarak jaivik hamalon kaa saamana kar sakati he

 Sanjeev Miglani believes that no research has yet been published in Ayurveda regarding the treatment of swine flu
 isliye is bare main zyada kuch nahin kaha ja saktaa
 But there is no need to panic from swine flu
 iskaa shikaar hue 85 fisadi marij 7 dinon ke bheetar prakritik pratirohak kshamta kii vajah se apane aap thik ho jate hai

 dow
 According to Miglani, taking care of a few things can prevent this disease - 01
 vitamin-si se bharpoor falon or hari patteydaar subjiyon kaa seven karen
 Take special care of cleanliness while cooking and eating
 02
 Place a tissue on the mouth and nose while coughing
 balgam behate pani main daalen
 03
 yadi parivaar main koi swine flu se peedit he to uske kapadon ko alag se rakhaa or dhoyaa jaae
 Do not touch the victim's nose and mouth
 04
 Wear a mask better than a doctor
 zyada logon se naa milen
 05
 rogi ke sampark main zyada naa aaen
 Pay attention to cleanliness at home
 06
 Avoid visiting public and crowded places
 logon se gale milane or chumban aadi karne se bachein
 07
 agar kisi vyakti ko lagaataar khaansee or chhinke aa rahi hon to usase kam se kam teen feet kii duuri par rahen

 When we started investigating in Uttarakhand, we got the idea right
 ye video uttarakhand main udhamsingh nagar ke bajpur shahar kaa he
 This is the petrol pump of Hindustan Petroleum Company
 hamane petrol pump ke karmchaariyon se sampark kiya
 The petrol pump worker and the owner of the pump said that yes, this video is from this petrol pump and it is not a one day affair but this monkey often comes here
 vah yahaan par sirf petrol ko chakhtaa, soonghta he or phir uchhal kud kar chalaa jaataa he! yah bandar kisi ko bhi koi nuksaan nahin pahunchaata he
 We have come to know that this monkey is stationed at the petrol pump, but why does this monkey taste petrol, why does it smell petrol by putting its mouth inside the tank? Before we tell you the truth of this monkey, also watch this viral video
 pichley saal oktober main haryana ke panipat main ek bandar parking main khadi motorcycle kaa pipe nikaalkar petrol pi rahaa tha, yahaan log pareshaan ho jate the ki aakhir unki bike kaa petrol kahaan gaayab ho jaataa he, video saamne aane ke baad petrol pine vaale bandar kaa khulaasa hua
 It is said that this monkey got so addicted to petrol that he did not eat even the best of things
 ab ham jaananaa chaahate the ki bandar or petrol kaa conection kya he
 Does the monkey really check the quality of petrol at the petrol pump, we talked to Vijendra Kumar Tyagi, the Chief Veterinary Officer of Ghaziabad about it, he told that petrol is made of hydro carbon, it also contains aromatic hydro carbon
 vah veporise karte hai
 It is clear from watching the video that this monkey is addicted to aromatic hydro carbon wappers and comes for the same again and again, he comes to smell it
 ab janata ye soch rahi he ki bandar jo he vah petrol kii gunvattta kii jaanch karne aa rahaa he, jabaki aisa nahin he or isamen koi shaq nahin he ki bandaron main sens of power bahut adhik hoti he, nakal karne kii aadat hoti he
 So, it is a case of addiction
 to is tarah petrol kii gunvattta jaanchane vaale bandar kii khabar viral test main fail hui
